TRIAL

<TRIAL_ID>

</TRIAL_ID>
<TRIAL_NAME>
You still cannot believe this is happening
</TRIAL_NAME>
<TRIAL_TYPE>
5
</TRIAL_TYPE>
<TRIAL_DESCRIPTION>
You still cannot believe this is happening… And yet, reality becomes enmeshed with mythology, in a sequence of surprises. You are facing Stymphalos, the mythical king of the area, son of Elatos and Laodice!  You ask him if he needs help ... "Not me" he answers... "the lake! Man's relationships with nature has been disrupted. A relationship that kept the lake of Stymphalia and the area around it almost unchanged for centuries…. The balance has been disrupted.  You will be my messenger, the emissary of the lake! And you will take our message throughout the whole world...There is large building on the shore of the lake, they call it "Museum". It has a wealth of information about the lake and its history, its environment, the people who lived here and their activities. Go and find out as much as you can...
</TRIAL_DESCRIPTION>

5
</TRIAL_TYPE>
<TRIAL_DESCRIPTION>
First you must learn about the land and the waters of Stymphalia.\\Go to the starting point of the exhibition and find the model that presents the erosion process of the rocks in the area, leading to the formation of the lake. TRIAL
</TRIAL>
<TRIAL_ID>
19
</TRIAL_ID>
<TRIAL_NAME>
The plants, the animals and the people in Lake Stymphalia.
</TRIAL_NAME>
<TRIAL_TYPE>
5
</TRIAL_TYPE>

<TRIAL_NAME>
An unknown farmer solved a series of problems
</TRIAL_NAME>
<TRIAL_TYPE>
5
</TRIAL_TYPE>
<TRIAL_DESCRIPTION>
An unknown farmer solved a series of problems during the cultivation of grains with a clever patent that is exhibited in the Museum. He managed to hold more in his arms in order to decrease the number of times he had to cross the field so as to load the cut grain before forming the sheaves. At the same time, he protected his hands from snake bites, since snakes had been hunting for rodents on the grain field. Locate the wooden object that he invented and type its name in the field "Keyword entry".

Just before the last one

<TRIAL_NAME>
King Stymphalos for Lake Stympahlia
</TRIAL_NAME>
<TRIAL_TYPE>
5
</TRIAL_TYPE>
<TRIAL_DESCRIPTION>
Now you can understand the concern of King Stymphalos for Lake Stympahlia and the message that you have to spread: humans and nature are directly connected, they influence each other and determine each other's fate in an intense and dynamic relationship. This is why people should always act with respect and prudence within the framework that is defined by the natural environment itself.This is your legacy from today's visit and these are the riches of the Environment Museum of Stymphalia. And don't forget your duty, to carry the message of these riches wherever you go!
</TRIAL_DESCRIPTION>
